<div id="sm-countdown-dialog" style="display:none">
    <p>El tiempo de espera expiró y las tarifas pueden haber cambiado</p>
    <div id="sm-countdown" style="display:none">19 Minutos 2 segundos</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    
    var HtmlHelpers = function() {
        return {
            getQueryStringValue: function(name) {
                var match = RegExp('[?&]' + name + '=([^&]*)').exec(window.location.search);
                var pal = /\+/g;
                return match && decodeURIComponent(match[1].replace( pal, ' '));
            }
        };
    }();

    
    var StringHelpers = function() {
        return {
            
            padLeft: function(string, padMask) {
                string = '' + string;
                return (padMask.substr(0, (padMask.length - string.length)) + string);
            }
        };
    }();

    
    var SessionManager = function()
    {
        var sessionTimeoutSeconds = HtmlHelpers.getQueryStringValue('ssc') || (1200),
            countdownSeconds = HtmlHelpers.getQueryStringValue('ssc') || (1200 ),
            $dlg,
            displayCountdownIntervalId,
            promptToExtendSessionTimeoutId,
            originalTitle = document.title;
        var t = function()
        {
            window.clearInterval(displayCountdownIntervalId);
            window.clearTimeout(promptToExtendSessionTimeoutId);
            sessionTimeoutSeconds = 10;
            startSessionManager();
        }
        var restartSession = function()
        {
            window.clearInterval(displayCountdownIntervalId);
            window.clearTimeout(promptToExtendSessionTimeoutId);
            sessionTimeoutSeconds = 2;
            startSessionManager();
        }

        var endSession = function()
        {
            $dlg.dialog('close');

            if (SessionManager.RedirectUrl != "")
            {
                if (SessionManager.SubDomain != "")
                    SessionManager.SubDomain = "http://" + SessionManager.SubDomain;
                window.location.href = SessionManager.SubDomain + SessionManager.RedirectUrl;
            }
            else
            {
                $.ajax({
                    type:"POST",
                    url:"/SparksVista/StickyRedirect",
                    data: { RedirectUrl : "" },
                    beforeSend: function () {
                        showWait();
                    },
                    success: function (urlRedirect) {
                        hideWait();
                        SessionManager.start();
                    }
                });
            }
        };
        var SessionSummary = function()
        {
            var existsSessionSummary = $("#SessionSummary").length > 0 ? "true" : "false";
            if (existsSessionSummary == "true")
            {
                // Tiempo restante de la session
                var existInput = $("#SessionSummary").find("input[name='ssc']").length;
                if ( !existInput )
                    $("#SessionSummary").append("<input type='hidden' name='ssc'>")

                if ( existInput )
                    $("input[name='ssc']").val(countdownSeconds);

                // Dominio para redirigir
                existInput = $("#SessionSummary").find("input[name='sssd']").length;
                if ( !existInput )
                {
                    $("#SessionSummary").append("<input type='hidden' name='sssd'>")
                    if (SessionManager.SubDomain=='') SessionManager.SubDomain = window.location.host;
                    $("input[name='sssd']").val(SessionManager.SubDomain);
                }
            }
        };
        var displayCountdown = function()
        {
            var countdown = function()
            {
                SessionSummary();
                var cd = new Date(countdownSeconds * 1000),
                    minutes = cd.getUTCMinutes(),
                    seconds = cd.getUTCSeconds(),
                    minutesDisplay = minutes === 1 ? '1 minuto ' : minutes === 0 ? '' : minutes + ' Minutos ',
                    secondsDisplay = seconds === 1 ? '1 segundo' : seconds + ' segundos' ;
                $('#sm-countdown').html(minutesDisplay + secondsDisplay);

                if (SessionManager.showTitleCounter == "true")
                    document.title = 'Inactivo en ' + StringHelpers.padLeft(minutes, '00') + ':' + StringHelpers.padLeft(seconds, '00');
                countdownSeconds--;
            };
            countdown();
            displayCountdownIntervalId = window.setInterval(countdown, 1000);
        };

        var promptToExtendSession = function() {
            if (SessionManager.showTitleCounter == "true")
                document.title = 'Atención, El tiempo de espera expiró y las tarifas pueden haber cambiado';
            $('#sm-countdown').html("");
            $("#btnDlgContinue").attr('disabled','disabled').addClass('ui-state-disabled').hide();
            $("div .ui-dialog-titlebar span#ui-id-2").replaceWith( "<h4 class='ui-dialog-title'>" + $("div .ui-dialog-titlebar span#ui-id-2").text() + "</h4>" );
            $("div .ui-dialog-titlebar span#ui-id-3").replaceWith( "<h4 class='ui-dialog-title'>" + $("div .ui-dialog-titlebar span#ui-id-3").text() + "</h4>" );
            $(".ui-dialog-buttonset button .ui-button-text" ).addClass( "btn kdo-button kdo-border-radius" );
            $("div .ui-dialog-titlebar" ).removeClass( "ui-widget-header" ).addClass("kdo-color-link--light");

            
            if (typeof Booking != 'undefined' && typeof Booking.RateRules != 'undefined' && typeof Booking.RateRules.Dlg != 'undefined')
            {
                Booking.RateRules.CloseDialog();
            }

            
            if (typeof Booking != 'undefined' && typeof Booking.DeepLink != 'undefined' && typeof Booking.DeepLink.divDeepLinkModal != 'undefined' && Booking.DeepLink.divDeepLinkModal.length)
            {
                Booking.DeepLink.divDeepLinkModal.fadeOut();
            }

            $dlg = $('#sm-countdown-dialog')
                .dialog({
                    title: 'Atención',
                    height: 250,
                    width: 350,
                    bgiframe: true,
                    modal: true,
                    buttons: [
                        {
                            id: "btnDlgRefresh",
                            text: "Actualizar Tarifas",
                            click: function() {
                                showWait();
                                endSession();
                            }
                        }]
                });
            SessionManager.Dlg = $dlg;
            window.clearInterval(displayCountdownIntervalId);
            window.clearTimeout(promptToExtendSessionTimeoutId);
            SessionManager.HideCloseButton();
        };


        var refreshSession = function() {
            window.clearInterval(displayCountdownIntervalId);
            window.clearTimeout(promptToExtendSessionTimeoutId);
            document.title = originalTitle;
            startSessionManager();
        };

        var startSessionManager = function() {
            promptToExtendSessionTimeoutId = window.setTimeout(promptToExtendSession, sessionTimeoutSeconds * 1000);
            countdownSeconds = sessionTimeoutSeconds;
            displayCountdown();
        };

        return {
            start: function() {
                startSessionManager();
            },
            extend: function() {
                refreshSession();
            },
            t: function() {
            t();
            },
            restartSession : function() {
                restartSession();
        }
        };
    }();

    SessionManager.RedirectUrl = "/Vuelos/Lista?af=9002298&ot=0&di=0&GAProd=AV&sd=2019-08-27&ed=2019-09-20&ib=LAP&ni=La Paz (LAP)&ob=ACA&no=Acapulco (ACA)&ti=round&ad1=2&ch1=1&ac1=3&";
    SessionManager.SubDomain = "";
    SessionManager.showTitleCounter = "false";

    SessionManager.GetRedirectUrl = function()
    {
        var urlHref = "http://" + SessionManager.SubDomain + SessionManager.RedirectUrl;
        return urlHref;
    }

    SessionManager.HideCloseButton = function () {
        $(".ui-dialog-titlebar-close").hide();
    }
    SessionManager.ShowCloseButton = function () {
        $(".ui-dialog-titlebar-close").show();
    }

    $(document).ready(function()
    {
        var enableStickySession = "true";
        if (enableStickySession == "true")
        {
            SessionManager.start();
        }
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
     $(document).ready(function () {
         
         if ($("#EtIATAob").val() != "") {
             $.ajax({
                 url: "/_Ajax/LocationtAirport",
                 type: "GET",
                 dataType: "json",
                 data: "ln=esp&term=" + $("#EtIATAob").val() + "",
                 contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
                 success: function (data) {
                     if (data != null && data.length > 0) {
                         var OutboundName = data[0].value;
                         if (!$("#EtCityOrig").val().match(OutboundName)) {
                             $("input[name='no']").val(OutboundName); 
                             Zion.fn.Products.Flight.PreserveSearchFormInfo($("input[name='no']"));
                         }
                     }
                     else {
                         $("#EtCityOrig").val("No se encontraron resultados");
                         $("#EtWthLea").val("0");
                     }
                 }
             });
         }

         
         if ($("#EtIATAib").val() != "") {
             $.ajax({
                 url: "/_Ajax/LocationtAirport",
                 type: "GET",
                 dataType: "json",
                 data: "ln=esp&term=" + $("#EtIATAib").val() + "",
                 contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
                 success: function (data) {
                     if (data != null && data.length > 0) {
                         var InboundName = data[0].value;
                         if (!$("#EtCityDest").val().match(InboundName)) {
                             
                             
                             $("input[name='ni']").val(InboundName)
                             Zion.fn.Products.Flight.PreserveSearchFormInfo($("input[name='ni']"));
                         }
                     }
                     else {
                         $("#EtCityDest").val("No se encontraron resultados");
                         $("#EtWthArr").val("0");
                     }
                 }
             });
         }

         
         $("#EtCityOrig").autocomplete({
             minLength: 3,
             delay: 500,
             source: function (request, response) {


                 $.ajax({
                     url: "//ajaxcore.e-tsw.com/getSearchJson.aspx",
                     dataType: "jsonp",
                     data: {
                         PalabraBuscada: request.term,
                         Lenguaje: "esp",
                         ItemTypes: "A:10",
                         Filters: "",
                         Af: "9002298"
                     },
                     beforeSend: function () {
                         $("#EtCityOrig").addClass("complete");
                     },
                     complete: function () {
                         $("#EtCityOrig").removeClass("complete");
                         $("#EtBxOrigin").css({ 'border': '' });
                     },
                     success: function (data) {
                         var arrayDestinations = new Array();
                         var object = new Object();
                         var DestId = "";
                         var filterCountryOrig = "";

                         
                         for (var a = 0; a < data.results.length; a++) {
                             object = data.results[a];
                             DestId = object.TypeID.toString().split('|')[1];
                             if (DestId != "") {
                                 if (filterCountryOrig) {
                                     if (filterCountryOrig.indexOf(object.Country) > -1) {
                                         arrayDestinations.push(object);
                                     }
                                 }
                                 else {
                                     arrayDestinations.push(object);
                                 }
                             }
                         }

                         if (!arrayDestinations.length) {
                             response($.map([{ "Label": "No se encontraron resultados" }], function (item) {
                                 return {
                                     id: "0",
                                     label: item.Label,
                                     value: item.Label,
                                     countryId: "0",
                                     typeId: "A|0",
                                     type: "A"
                                 }
                             }));
                         }
                         else {
                             response($.map(arrayDestinations, function (item) {
                                 return {
                                     id: item.ID,
                                     label: item.Label,
                                     value: item.Label,
                                     countryId: item.Country,
                                     typeId: item.TypeID,
                                     type: item.Type
                                 }
                             }));
                         }
                     }
                 });
             },
             select: function (event, iu) {
                 
                 var Name = iu.item.value.toString().substring(0, iu.item.value.toString().indexOf(')') + 1);;
                 var IATA = iu.item.typeId.toString().split('|')[0];
                 $("#EtIATAob").val(IATA); 
                 Zion.fn.Products.Flight.PreserveSearchFormInfo($("#EtIATAob")); 
                 $("#EtWthLea").val("1");
                 $("#EtIATAno").val(Name.substring(0, iu.item.value.toString().indexOf(')')));
                 $("#EtCityOrig").addClass("EtSelect");
                 $("#EtBxOrigin").css({ 'border': '' });
             },
             focus: function () {
                 return false;
             },
             open: function (event, iu) {
                 
             }
         }).data("ui-autocomplete")._renderItem = function (ul, item) {
             var flagImage;
             flagImage = (item.countryId != "") ? "<img src='//images.e-tsw.com/_lib/vimages/Flags/" + (item.countryId == '0' ? 'all' : item.countryId) + ".gif' /> " : "";
             item.value2 = item.value.replace(new RegExp("(?![^&;]+;)(?!<[^<>]*)(" + $.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(this.term) + ")(?![^<>]*>)(?![^&;]+;)", "gi"), "<strong>$1</strong>");
             return $("<li></li>").data("item.autocomplete", item)
                 .append($("<a></a>, ").html(flagImage + "<span class='EtSpCtAc'>" + item.value2 + "</span>"))
                 .appendTo(ul);
         }

         

         
         $("#EtCityDest").autocomplete({
             minLength: 3,
             delay: 500,
             source: function (request, response) {


                 $.ajax({
                     url: "//ajaxcore.e-tsw.com/getSearchJson.aspx",
                     dataType: "jsonp",
                     data: {
                         PalabraBuscada: request.term,
                         Lenguaje: "esp",
                         ItemTypes: "A:10",
                         Filters: "",
                         Af: "9002298"
                     },
                     beforeSend: function () {
                         $("#EtCityDest").addClass("complete");
                     },
                     complete: function () {
                         $("#EtCityDest").removeClass("complete");
                     },
                     success: function (data) {
                         var arrayDestinations = new Array();
                         var object = new Object();
                         var DestId = "";
                         var filterCountryDest = "";

                         
                         for (var a = 0; a < data.results.length; a++) {
                             object = data.results[a];
                             DestId = object.TypeID.toString().split('|')[1];
                             if (DestId != "") {
                                 if (filterCountryDest) {
                                     if (filterCountryDest.indexOf(object.Country) > -1) {
                                         arrayDestinations.push(object);
                                     }
                                 }
                                 else {
                                     arrayDestinations.push(object);
                                 }
                             }
                         }

                         if (!arrayDestinations.length) {
                             response($.map([{ "Label": "No se encontraron resultados" }], function (item) {
                                 return {
                                     id: "0",
                                     label: item.Label,
                                     value: item.Label,
                                     countryId: "0",
                                     typeId: "A|0",
                                     type: "A"
                                 }
                             }));
                         }
                         else {
                             response($.map(arrayDestinations, function (item) {
                                 return {
                                     id: item.ID,
                                     label: item.Label,
                                     value: item.Label,
                                     countryId: item.Country,
                                     typeId: item.TypeID,
                                     type: item.Type
                                 }
                             }));
                         }
                     }
                 });
             },
             select: function (event, iu) {
                 
                 var Name = iu.item.value.toString().substring(0, iu.item.value.toString().indexOf(')') + 1);
                 var IATA = iu.item.typeId.toString().split('|')[0];
                 $("#EtIATAib").val(IATA); 
                 Zion.fn.Products.Flight.PreserveSearchFormInfo($("#EtIATAib")); 
                 $("#EtWthArr").val("1");
                 $("#EtIATAni").val(Name.substring(0, iu.item.value.toString().indexOf(')')));
                 $("#EtCityDest").addClass("EtSelect");
                 $("#Etdt").val(iu.item.id);
                 $("#EtBxDestiny").css({ 'border': '' });
             },
             focus: function () {
                 return false;
             },
             open: function (event, iu) {
                 
             }
         }).data("ui-autocomplete")._renderItem = function (ul, item) {
             var flagImage;
             flagImage = (item.countryId != "") ? "<img src='//images.e-tsw.com/_lib/vimages/Flags/" + (item.countryId == '0' ? 'all' : item.countryId) + ".gif' /> " : "";
             item.value2 = item.value.replace(new RegExp("(?![^&;]+;)(?!<[^<>]*)(" + $.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex(this.term) + ")(?![^<>]*>)(?![^&;]+;)", "gi"), "<strong>$1</strong>");
             return $("<li></li>").data("item.autocomplete", item)
                 .append($("<a></a>, ").html(flagImage + "<span class='EtSpCtAc'>" + item.value2 + "</span>"))
                 .appendTo(ul);
         };
         });
</script>

    <div id="FlightFilterBox" style="display:block;" data-showfilters="1">
<script type="text/javascript">

    $(document).ready(function () {

        $("#StartPrice").val(991598);
        $("#EndPrice").val(1259501);

        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.MinPrice = 991598 ;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.MaxPrice = 1259501 ;

        
        $("#EtPriceRange").slider({
            range: true, min: 991598, max: 1259501, values: [991598, 1259501], step: 100,
            slide: function(event, ui) {
                var selectedMin = ui.values[0];
                var selectedMax = ui.values[1];
                if (selectedMax <= selectedMin )  { return false; } 
                $("#EtpriceRangeMin").html("De:<label> $ " + selectedMin);
                $("#EtpriceRangeMax").html("A:<label> $ " + selectedMax);
                $("#StartPrice").val(ui.values[0]);
                $("#EndPrice").val(ui.values[1]);
                
                Zion.fn.Products.Flight.LoadFlightFilters();
                Zion.fn.Products.Flight.ApplyFlightFilters(this);
            },
            stop: function(event, ui) { },
            start: function(event, ui) { Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightFilters(); }
        });
        $("#EtpriceRangeMin").html("De:<label> $ 991598");
        $("#EtpriceRangeMax").html("A:<label> $ 1259501");

        
        $(".FlightOutboundScheduleFilter,.FlightInboundScheduleFilter").click(function ()
        {
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.LoadFlightFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.ApplyFlightFilters(this);
        });

        
        $("#DirectInFlightFilter,#ScaledInFlightFilter,#DirectOutFlightFilter,#ScaledOutFlightFilter").click(function ()
        {
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.LoadFlightFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.ApplyFlightFilters(this);
        });

        
        $(".FlightInAirlineFilters,.FlightOutAirlineFilters").click(function ()
        {
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.LoadFlightFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.ApplyFlightFilters(this);
        });

        
        $("#ClearFlightFilters,.clearFilters").click(function(e) {
            showWait();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightGUIFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.LoadFlightFilters();
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.ApplyFlightFilters();
            hideWait();
        });

        
    });

    
    function ShowMatchingResults() { $("#FlightMatchingResults").html(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.TotalMatches); }

    
    function HideLazyLoader()
    {
        
        if ($(".Et_flightListWrapper:visible").length == 0) $("#msgError").show(); else  $("#msgError").hide();

        
        if ($(".Et_flightListWrapper:visible").length >= Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.TotalMatches )  $(".Et_addons_LoadMoreProducts.Flight").css("display", "none");
        else  $(".Et_addons_LoadMoreProducts.Flight").css("display", "block");
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters =
    {
        "AirlineOutIds": null,          
        "AirlineInIds": null,           
        "ShowOutDirectFlights": null,   
        "ShowInDirectFlights": null,    
        "ShowOutScaledFlights": null ,  
        "ShowInScaledFlights": null ,   
        "InboundSchedule": null,        
        "OutboundSchedule": null,       
        "MaxPrice": 0,                  
        "MinPrice": 0,                  
        "TotalMatches": 0,              
        "FinalMaxPrice": 1259501,     
        "FinalMinPrice": 991598,   
        "SelectedFilter": null,         
    };

    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination =
    {
        "NumPage": 1,                   
        "TotalPeerPage": 15,            
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightGUIFilters = function()
    {

        
        $(".FlightOutAirlineFilters").each(function () { 
            $('#' + this.value).prop('checked', false);
        });
        $(".FlightInAirlineFilters").each(function () {
            $('#' + this.value).prop('checked', false);
        });

        
        if ($("#DirectFlightFilter").is(":visible")) $("#DirectFlightFilter").prop('checked', true);

        if ($("#ScaledFlightFilter").is(":visible"))  $("#ScaledFlightFilter").prop('checked', true);

        
        $('#EtPriceRange').slider( "option", "min", Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.FinalMinPrice );
        $('#EtPriceRange').slider( "option", "max", Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.FinalMaxPrice );
        $('#EtPriceRange').slider( "values", [ Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.FinalMinPrice, Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.FinalMaxPrice] );
        $("#StartPrice").val(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.FinalMinPrice);
        $("#EndPrice").val(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.FinalMaxPrice);

        
        $(".FlightOutboundScheduleFilter").prop('checked', false);

        
        $(".FlightInboundScheduleFilter").prop('checked', false);

        
        $("select#FlightOrderList").val('0');
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightFilters = function()
    {

        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByOutAirline");
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByInAirline");
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByDirectOutFlights");
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByScaledOutFlights");
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByDirectInFlights");
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByScaledInFlights");
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByPrice");
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByOutboundSchedule");
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").removeClass("ShowByInboundSchedule");

        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.NumPage = 1;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.TotalPeerPage = 15;

        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds = null;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds = null;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights = null;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights = null;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights = null;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights = null;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule = null;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule = null;
        //Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.MaxPrice = 0;
        //Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.MinPrice = 0;
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter = null;

        //  - Oculta filtros dinamicos
        $("#DynamicFlightFilterOptions").hide();
        $(".filter-option-dynamic").hide();
        
        $(".FlightOutAirlineFilters").each(function () {
            if($("." + this.value).length > 0)
            {
                $('#' + this.value).show();
                $('label[for="'+ this.value +'"]').show();
            }
            else
            {
                $('#' + this.value).hide();
                $('label[for="'+ this.value +'"]').hide();
            }
        });

        
        $(".FlightInAirlineFilters").each(function () {
            if($("." + this.value).length > 0)
            {
                $('#' + this.value).show();
                $('label[for="'+ this.value +'"]').show();
            }
            else
            {
                $('#' + this.value).hide();
                $('label[for="'+ this.value +'"]').hide();
            }
        });
    }


    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.LoadFlightFilters = function ()
    {
        
        var airlineIds = new Array();
        $(".FlightOutAirlineFilters").each(function () { 
            if (this.checked)
                airlineIds.push(this.value);
        });
        if (airlineIds.length == 0)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds = null;
        else
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds = airlineIds;
        
        airlineIds = new Array();
        $(".FlightInAirlineFilters").each(function () { 
            if (this.checked)
                airlineIds.push(this.value);
        });
        if (airlineIds.length == 0)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds = null;
        else
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds = airlineIds;

        
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.MinPrice = $("#StartPrice").val();
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.MaxPrice = $("#EndPrice").val();

        
        
        if ($("#DirectOutFlightFilter").is(":visible")) {
            var show =  $("#DirectOutFlightFilter").is(":checked") ;
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights = show == false ? null : show ;
        } else Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights = null; 
        
        if ($("#DirectInFlightFilter").is(":visible")) {
            var show =   $("#DirectInFlightFilter").is(":checked") ;
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights = show == false ? null : show ;
        } else Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights = null; 
        
        if ($("#ScaledOutFlightFilter").is(":visible")) {
            show =   $("#ScaledOutFlightFilter").is(":checked") ;
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights = show == false ? null : show ;
        }else Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights = null; 
        
        if ($("#ScaledInFlightFilter").is(":visible")) {
            show = $("#ScaledInFlightFilter").is(":checked") ;
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights = show == false ? null : show ;
        }else Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights = null; 

        
        
        var outScheduleFiltersId = new Array();
        $(".FlightOutboundScheduleFilter").each(function () {
            if (this.checked)
                outScheduleFiltersId.push(this.value);
        });
        if (outScheduleFiltersId.length == 0)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule = null;
        else
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule = outScheduleFiltersId;

        
        
        var inScheduleFiltersId = new Array();
        $(".FlightInboundScheduleFilter").each(function () {
            if (this.checked)
                inScheduleFiltersId.push(this.value);
        });
        if (inScheduleFiltersId.length == 0)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule = null;
        else
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule = inScheduleFiltersId;

        return Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters;
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.ApplyFlightFilters = function (selectedfilter)
    {

        if ( typeof selectedfilter != "undefined" && selectedfilter.className != "")
        {
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter = selectedfilter.className;
        }

        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds != null || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds != null )
        {

            
            $( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds ).each(function (index, value) {
                $("." + value ).addClass("ShowByOutAirline");
            });

            
            $( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds ).each(function (index, value) {
                $("." + value ).addClass("ShowByInAirline");
            });

        }else
        {
            
            $("div.Flight.ProductBox").addClass("ShowByOutAirline");
            $("div.Flight.ProductBox").addClass("ShowByInAirline");
        }


        
        
        if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights != null && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights == true )
            $(".OutD").addClass("ShowByDirectOutFlights");
        
        if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights != null && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights == true)
            $(".OutS").addClass("ShowByScaledOutFlights");
        
        if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights != null && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights == true )
            $(".InD").addClass("ShowByDirectInFlights");
        
        if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights != null && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights == true)
            $(".InS").addClass("ShowByScaledInFlights");

        
        $(".ProductBox").each(function(i,n){
            var precio=parseInt($(this).find(".price").val());
            var minimo=parseInt( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.MinPrice );
            var maximo=parseInt( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.MaxPrice );
            if (precio >= 0) {
                if ( (precio >= minimo) && (precio <= maximo))
                    $(this).addClass("ShowByPrice");
                else
                    $(this).removeClass("ShowByPrice");
            }
        });

        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule != null )
        {
            
            
            if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule.length == 0 )
                $("div.Flight.ProductBox").addClass("ShowByOutboundSchedule");
            else
            {
                
                $(".ProductBox").each(function(index,obj)
                {
                    var productBox = $(this);
                    var scheduleId = productBox.find(".OutboundScheduleId").val();
                    
                    $( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule ).each(function (index, value) {
                        if ( scheduleId == value )
                        {
                            productBox.addClass("ShowByOutboundSchedule");
                            return false;
                        }
                    });
                });
            }
        }else
            
            $("div.Flight.ProductBox").addClass("ShowByOutboundSchedule");

        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule != null )
        {
            
            
            if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule.length == 0 )
                $("div.Flight.ProductBox").addClass("ShowByInboundSchedule");
            else
            {
                
                $(".ProductBox").each(function(index,obj)
                {
                    var productBox = $(this);
                    var scheduleId = productBox.find(".InboundScheduleId").val();
                    
                    $( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule ).each(function (index, value) {
                        if ( scheduleId == value )
                        {
                            productBox.addClass("ShowByInboundSchedule");
                            return false; 
                        }
                    });
                });
            }
        }else
            
            $("div.Flight.ProductBox").addClass("ShowByInboundSchedule");

        
        ApplyFlightFilters();
        
        ShowDynamicFilters();
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.UpdateCountersFlightFilters = function(filteredFlights)
    {
        
        if(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != null && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter.indexOf("ui-slider") < 0)
        {
            var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("PriceRange");
            totalFlights = totalFlights.sort(SortByPriceDesc);
            var minimo = parseFloat(totalFlights.find(".FlightOrderBoxByPrice")[0].value) - 1;
            var maximo = parseFloat(totalFlights.find(".FlightOrderBoxByPrice")[totalFlights.length - 1].value) + 1;
            $('#EtPriceRange').slider( "option", "min", minimo );
            $('#EtPriceRange').slider( "option", "max", maximo );
            $("#EtpriceRangeMin").html("De:<label> $ " + minimo);
            $("#EtpriceRangeMax").html("A:<label> $ " + maximo);
            if((maximo - minimo) < 100)
            {
                $( "#EtPriceRange" ).slider( "option", "disabled", true );
            }else {
                $( "#EtPriceRange" ).slider( "option", "disabled", false );
            }
        }

        
        if(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != "DirectOutFlightFilter"
            && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != "ScaledOutFlightFilter"
            || ($(".DirectOutFlightFilter").filter('input:checked').length
              + $(".ScaledOutFlightFilter").filter('input:checked').length) == 0)
        {
            var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("ScaledOut");
            var totald = $( totalFlights ).filter('.OutD').length;
            if(totald > 0)
            {
                $('#DirectOutFlightFilter').prop('disabled', false);
                $('label[for="DirectOutFlightFilter"] span').html(totald);
            }
            else
            {
                $('#DirectOutFlightFilter').prop('checked', false);
                $('label[for="DirectOutFlightFilter"] span').html(0);
                $('#DirectOutFlightFilter').prop('disabled', true);
            }

            var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("ScaledOut");
            var totals = $( totalFlights ).filter('.OutS').length;
            if(totals > 0)
            {
                $('#ScaledOutFlightFilter').prop('disabled', false);
                $('label[for="ScaledOutFlightFilter"] span').html(totals);
            }
            else
            {
                $('#ScaledOutFlightFilter').prop('checked', false);
                $('label[for="ScaledOutFlightFilter"] span').html(0);
                $('#ScaledOutFlightFilter').prop('disabled', true);
            }
        }

        
        if(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != "DirectInFlightFilter"
            && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != "ScaledInFlightFilter"
            || ($(".DirectInFlightFilter").filter('input:checked').length
              + $(".ScaledInFlightFilter").filter('input:checked').length) == 0)
        {
            var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("ScaledIn");
            var totald = $( totalFlights ).filter('.InD').length;
            if(totald > 0)
            {
                $('#DirectInFlightFilter').prop('disabled', false);
                $('label[for="DirectInFlightFilter"] span').html(totald);
            }
            else
            {
                $('#DirectInFlightFilter').prop('checked', false);
                $('label[for="DirectInFlightFilter"] span').html(0);
                $('#DirectInFlightFilter').prop('disabled', true);
            }

            var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("ScaledIn");
            var totals = $( totalFlights ).filter('.InS').length;
            if(totals > 0)
            {
                $('#ScaledInFlightFilter').prop('disabled', false);
                $('label[for="ScaledInFlightFilter"] span').html(totals);
            }
            else
            {
                $('#ScaledInFlightFilter').prop('checked', false);
                $('label[for="ScaledInFlightFilter"] span').html(0);
                $('#ScaledInFlightFilter').prop('disabled', true);
            }
        }

        
        if(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != "FlightOutboundScheduleFilter"
           || $(".FlightOutboundScheduleFilter").filter('input:checked').length == 0)
            $(".FlightOutboundScheduleFilter").each(function () {
                var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("ScheduleOut");
                var total = $( totalFlights ).find('.OutboundScheduleId[value="'+ this.value +'"]').length;
                if(total > 0)
                {
                    $('#FlightOutboundScheduleFilter'+ this.value).prop('disabled', false);
                    $('label[for="Out_'+ this.value +'"] span').html(total);
                }
                else
                {
                    $('#FlightOutboundScheduleFilter'+ this.value).prop('checked', false);
                    $('label[for="Out_'+ this.value +'"] span').html(0);
                    $('#FlightOutboundScheduleFilter'+ this.value).prop('disabled', true);
                }
            });

        
        if(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != "FlightInboundScheduleFilter"
           || $(".FlightInboundScheduleFilter").filter('input:checked').length == 0)
            $(".FlightInboundScheduleFilter").each(function () {
                var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("ScheduleIn");
                var total = $( totalFlights ).find('.InboundScheduleId[value="'+ this.value +'"]').length;
                if(total > 0)
                {
                    $('#FlightInboundScheduleFilter'+ this.value).prop('disabled', false);
                    $('label[for="In_'+ this.value +'"] span').html(total);
                }
                else
                {
                    $('#FlightInboundScheduleFilter'+ this.value).prop('checked', false);
                    $('label[for="In_'+ this.value +'"] span').html(0);
                    $('#FlightInboundScheduleFilter'+ this.value).prop('disabled', true);
                }
            });

        
        if(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != "FlightOutAirlineFilters"
            || $(".FlightOutAirlineFilters").filter('input:checked').length == 0)
            $(".FlightOutAirlineFilters").each(function () {
                var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("OutAirline");
                var total = $( totalFlights ).filter("." + this.value).length;
                if(total > 0)
                {
                    $('#' + this.value).prop('disabled', false);
                    $('label[for="'+ this.value +'"] span').html(total);
                }
                else
                {
                    $('#' + this.value).prop('checked', false);
                    $('label[for="'+ this.value +'"] span').html(0);
                    $('#' + this.value).prop('disabled', true);
                }
            });

        
        if(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.SelectedFilter != "FlightInAirlineFilters"
            || $(".FlightInAirlineFilters").filter('input:checked').length == 0)
            $(".FlightInAirlineFilters").each(function () {
                var totalFlights = GetTotalForFilter("InAirline");
                var total = $( totalFlights ).filter("." + this.value).length;
                if(total > 0)
                {
                    $('#' + this.value).prop('disabled', false);
                    $('label[for="'+ this.value +'"] span').html(total);
                }
                else
                {
                    $('#' + this.value).prop('checked', false);
                    $('label[for="'+ this.value +'"] span').html(0);
                    $('#' + this.value).prop('disabled', true);
                }
            });

    }

    
    function GetTotalForFilter(filterExcluded)
    {
        var totalFlights = $("div.Flight.ProductBox"); 

        
        if (filterExcluded != "ScaledOut"
            && (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights != null
            && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights == true
            || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights != null
            && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights == true))
            totalFlights = $( totalFlights ).filter(".ShowByDirectOutFlights , .ShowByScaledOutFlights"); 

        
        if (filterExcluded != "ScaledIn"
            && (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights != null
            && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights == true
            || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights != null
            && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights == true))
            totalFlights = $( totalFlights ).filter(".ShowByDirectInFlights , .ShowByScaledInFlights"); 

        
        if (filterExcluded != "OutAirline" && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds != null )
            totalFlights = $( totalFlights ).filter(".ShowByOutAirline"); 

        
        if (filterExcluded != "InAirline" && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds != null)
            totalFlights = $( totalFlights ).filter(".ShowByInAirline"); 

        
        if(filterExcluded != "ScheduleOut" && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule != null )
            totalFlights = $( totalFlights ).filter(".ShowByOutboundSchedule"); 

        
        if(filterExcluded != "ScheduleIn" && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule != null )
            totalFlights = $( totalFlights ).filter(".ShowByInboundSchedule"); 

        
        if(filterExcluded != "PriceRange")
        totalFlights = $(totalFlights).filter(".ShowByPrice");

        return totalFlights;
    }

    
    function ShowDynamicFilters()
    {
        var showFilters = false;

        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds != null || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds != null )
        {
            
            $( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds ).each(function (index, value) {
                showFilters = true;
                $("#DynamicAirline" + value).show();
            });

            
            $( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds ).each(function (index, value) {
                showFilters = true;
                $("#DynamicAirline" + value).show();
            });
        }

        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule != null &&  Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule.length > 0)
        {
            showFilters = true;
            
            $( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule ).each(function (index, value) {
                $("#FlightOutboundScheduleFilterDynamic" + value).show();
            });
        }

        
        if( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule != null &&  Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule.length > 0)
        {
            showFilters = true;
            
            $( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule ).each(function (index, value) {
                $("#FlightInboundScheduleFilterDynamic" + value).show();
            });
        }

        
        
        if ( ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights != null || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights != null ||
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights != null || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights != null) &&
            (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights == true || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights == true ||
            (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights == true || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights == true )   )
            )
        {
            if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights != null  && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights == true)
            {
                showFilters = true;
                $("#DirectOutFlightFilterDynamic").show();
            } 

            if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights != null  && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights == true)
            {
                $("#ScaledOutFlightFilterDynamic").show();
                showFilters = true;
            } 

            if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights != null  && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights == true)
            {
                $("#DirectInFlightFilterDynamic").show();
                showFilters = true;
            }

            if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights != null  && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights == true)
            {
                $("#ScaledInFlightFilterDynamic").show();
                showFilters = true;
            }

        }


        
        if (showFilters)
            $("#DynamicFlightFilterOptions").show();
        else
            $("#DynamicFlightFilterOptions").hide();

    }


    function ApplyFlightFilters()
    {
        $("div.Flight.ProductBox").css("display", "none");
        ShowFlights( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.NumPage * Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.TotalPeerPage );
    }

    
    function ShowFlights(maxToShow) {

        var count = 1;
        var filteredFlights = $("div.Flight.ProductBox"); 

        
        if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineOutIds != null )
            filteredFlights = $( filteredFlights ).filter(".ShowByOutAirline"); 
        
        if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.AirlineInIds != null)
            filteredFlights = $( filteredFlights ).filter(".ShowByInAirline"); 

        
        
        if ( ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights != null || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights != null ||
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights != null || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights != null) &&
            (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights == true || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights == true ||
            (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights == true || Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights == true )   )
            )
        {
            var scaledFilters = new Array();
            var scaledFiltersString = "";

            if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights != null  && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutDirectFlights == true)
                scaledFilters.push( ".ShowByDirectOutFlights" ) ; 

            if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights != null  && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowOutScaledFlights == true)
                scaledFilters.push( ".ShowByScaledOutFlights" ); 

            $( scaledFilters ).each( function( index, item )
            {
                if ( index < scaledFilters.length - 1 )
                    scaledFiltersString += item + ",";
                else
                    scaledFiltersString += item;
            });

            
            if ( scaledFiltersString != "" )
                filteredFlights = $(filteredFlights).filter(scaledFiltersString); 

            scaledFiltersString = "";
            scaledFilters = new Array();

            if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights != null  && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInDirectFlights == true)
                scaledFilters.push( ".ShowByDirectInFlights" ); 

            if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights != null  && Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.ShowInScaledFlights == true)
                scaledFilters.push( ".ShowByScaledInFlights" ); 

            $( scaledFilters ).each( function( index, item )
            {
                if ( index < scaledFilters.length - 1 )
                    scaledFiltersString += item + ",";
                else
                    scaledFiltersString += item;
            });

            
            if ( scaledFiltersString != "" )
                filteredFlights = $(filteredFlights).filter(scaledFiltersString); 
        }

        
        filteredFlights = $(filteredFlights).filter(".ShowByPrice");

        
        if( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.OutboundSchedule != null )
            filteredFlights = $( filteredFlights ).filter(".ShowByOutboundSchedule"); 

        
        if( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.InboundSchedule != null )
            filteredFlights = $( filteredFlights ).filter(".ShowByInboundSchedule"); 

        
        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.UpdateCountersFlightFilters(filteredFlights);

        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.TotalMatches=0;
        $( filteredFlights ).each(function (index, obj) {
            if (count <= maxToShow) {
                if ( Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Animation.showAnimatedFlightListResults )
                    $(this).show('slow');
                else
                    $(this).show();
            }
            count++;
        });

        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Filters.TotalMatches = count-1;
        ShowMatchingResults();
        HideLazyLoader();
    }


</script>

    function getFlightOutboundSegmentsParams( idBlockOut )
    {
        var inputs = $("#" + idBlockOut + "_SegOut").children();
        var segmentsParams = "";

        $.each(inputs, function (index, obj){
            segmentsParams+= obj.name + "=" + obj.value;
            if( index+1 != inputs.length )
                segmentsParams+= "&";
        });

        
        segmentsParams += "&frk=" + $("#" + idBlockOut + "Out_RateKey").val();
        segmentsParams += "&fqi=" + $("input[name='" + idBlockOut + "Out']").val();

        return segmentsParams;
    }

    $(document).ready(function ()
    {

        
        $("body").on("click", ".EtBtnReservationOutbound", function()
        {

            var blockId = $(this).attr("id"); 
            var quoteKeyBlockOut = $("#" + blockId + "Out_ApiId").val();
            var idBlockOut = $("input[name='" + blockId + "Out']").attr("id");  

            if ( typeof quoteKeyBlockOut != 'undefined' )
                if (quoteKeyBlockOut)
                {
                    $("input[name='fido']").val(quoteKeyBlockOut);
                    $("input[name='ii']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_IdAir").val());
                    $("input[name='ao']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_NameAir").val());
                    $("input[name='sd']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_StartDate").val());
                    $("input[name='ed']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_EndDate").val());
                    $("input[name='st']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_StartTime").val());
                    $("input[name='et']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_EndTime").val());
                    $("input[name='rt']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_TotalRate").val());
                    $("input[name='gt']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_GrossTotal").val());
                    $("input[name='da']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_DutyAmount").val());
                    $("input[name='pcid']").val($("#" + idBlockOut + "_pcid").val());

                
                    var segmentsParams = getFlightOutboundSegmentsParams( blockId );

                    
                    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.FlightListInboundQuote( segmentsParams );

                }
                else
                {   
                    alert("Seleccionar ida");
                }
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting =
    {
        OrderByPrice: 0,
        OrderByDuration: 1,
        OrderByStops: 2,
        OrderByDepartureTime: 3,
        OrderByArrivalTime: 4
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortFlights = function () {
         
        var flightOrderList = document.getElementById("FlightOrderList");

        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.OrderByPrice == flightOrderList.selectedIndex)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByPrice();
        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.OrderByDuration == flightOrderList.selectedIndex)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByDuration();
        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.OrderByStops == flightOrderList.selectedIndex)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByStops();
        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.OrderByDepartureTime == flightOrderList.selectedIndex)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByDepartureTime();
        
        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.OrderByArrivalTime == flightOrderList.selectedIndex)
            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByArrivalTime();

        
                Zion.fn.Products.Flight.CleanFlightFilters();
                        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.LoadFlightFilters();
                        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.ApplyFlightFilters();
    }

  
    function SortByPriceDesc(a, b) {
        var priceA = parseInt($(a).find(".FlightOrderBoxByPrice").val());
        var priceB = parseInt($(b).find(".FlightOrderBoxByPrice").val());
        if (priceA < priceB)
            return -1;
        else if (priceA > priceB)
            return 1;
        else
            return 0;
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByPrice = function () {
        var ProductBox = $(".Flight.ProductBox");
        var ProductBoxPrice = ProductBox.sort(SortByPriceDesc);
        $("#FlightListOrderedBox").html("");
        $("#FlightListOrderedBox").html(ProductBoxPrice);
    }

 
    function SortByDurationDesc(a, b) {
        var durationA = parseInt($(a).find(".FlightOrderBoxByDuration").val());
        var durationB = parseInt($(b).find(".FlightOrderBoxByDuration").val());
        if (durationA < durationB)
            return -1;
        else if (durationA > durationB)
            return 1;
        else
            return 0;
    }

     
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByDuration = function () {
        var ProductBox = $(".Flight.ProductBox");
        var ProductBoxDuration = ProductBox.sort(SortByDurationDesc);
        $("#FlightListOrderedBox").html("");
        $("#FlightListOrderedBox").html(ProductBoxDuration);
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByStops = function () {
        var ProductBox = $(".Flight.ProductBox");
        var ProductBoxStops = ProductBox.sort(SortByStopsDesc);
        $("#FlightListOrderedBox").html("");
        $("#FlightListOrderedBox").html(ProductBoxStops);
    }

        var stopA = parseInt($(a).find(".FlightOrderBoxByStops").val());
        var stopB = parseInt($(b).find(".FlightOrderBoxByStops").val());
        if (stopA < stopB)
            return -1;
        else if (stopA > stopB)
            return 1;
        else
            return 0;
    }

    
    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Sorting.ShortByDepartureTime = function () {
        var ProductBox = $(".Flight.ProductBox");
        var ProductBoxDeparture = ProductBox.sort(SortByDepartureTimeDesc);
        $("#FlightListOrderedBox").html("");
        $("#FlightListOrderedBox").html(ProductBoxDeparture);

    }

   
    function SortByDepartureTimeDesc(a, b) {
        var depTimeA = $(a).find(".FlightOrderBoxByDepartureTime").val();
        var depTimeB = $(b).find(".FlightOrderBoxByDepartureTime").val();
        if (depTimeA < depTimeB)
            return -1;

            return 1;

    }

            <script type="text/javascript">
            $(document).ready(function () {

                
                $(window).scroll(function () {
                    if ($(window).scrollTop() + $(window).height() == $(document).height()) {
                        if (Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Animation.isAutoLazyLoaderEnabled) {
                            Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.NumPage++;
                            ShowFlights(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.NumPage * Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.TotalPeerPage);
                        }
                    }
                });

                $(".Et_addons_LoadMoreProducts.Flight").click(function () {
                    Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.NumPage++;
                    ShowFlights(Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.NumPage * Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Pagination.TotalPeerPage);
                });
            });
            </script>

        function copyToResume() {
            $("#noAdultsResume").html($("#EtNumAdults").val());
            $("#noKidsResume").html($("#EtNumChild").val());
            var arrFromDate = $("#EtDateFromFlightISO").val().split("-");
            var fromDate = new Date(arrFromDate[0], parseInt(arrFromDate[1])-1, parseInt(arrFromDate[2]));
            fromDate = $.datepicker.formatDate("dd MM yy", fromDate);
            $("#fromDateResume").html(fromDate);
            if($("#EtRdoFlightRound").is(":checked")){
                var arrToDate = $("#EtDateToFlightISO").val().split("-");
                var toDate = new Date(arrToDate[0], parseInt(arrToDate[1]) - 1, parseInt(arrToDate[2]));
                toDate = $.datepicker.formatDate("dd MM yy", toDate);
                $("#toDateResume").html(" - "+toDate);
            }else{
                $("#toDateResume").html("");
            }
            $("#fromIATAResume").html($("#EtIATAob").val());
            $("#toIATAResume").html($("#EtIATAib").val());
        }

        $(document).ready(function ()
        {
            
            $("#BtnSearchFlights").click(function()
            {
                tripInformation =  $("input[name = 'ti']:checked").val();
                if (ValidateFligthSearchForm()) {
                    if (tripInformation == "one" )
                        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.SearchTuplesFlights(); 
                    else
                        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.FlightListOutboundQuote(); 
                    
                    $("#flightSearchBox").hide();
                    copyToResume();
                    $("#searchSummary").show();
                }
            });
            $("#searchSummary").click(function(){
                $("#flightSearchBox").show();
                $("#searchSummary").hide();
            });
            
            InitializateFlightChildSearchForm();

            if ( !ValidateFligthSearchForm() ) 
            {
                
                Zion.fn.Products.Flight.FlightSuggestedQuote('M', Zion.fn.Products.Flight.Model.FirstModel.ModelData);
            }
            else
            {
                
                tripInformation =  $("input[name = 'ti']:checked").val();
                if (ValidateFligthSearchForm()) {
                    if (tripInformation == "one" )
                        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.SearchTuplesFlights(); 
                    else
                        Zion.fn.Products.Flight.FlightListOutboundQuote(); 
                    
                    $("#flightSearchBox").hide();
                    copyToResume();
                    $("#searchSummary").show();
                }
            }
            
            $("#EtFlightProduct").on("click",".leftControl",function(){
                var lista = $(this).parent();
                lista.data("index",parseInt(lista.data("index"))-1);
                slidePayments(lista.data("index"),$(this).parent());
            });
            $("#EtFlightProduct").on("click",".rightControl",function(){
                var lista = $(this).parent();
                lista.data("index",parseInt(lista.data("index"))+1);
                slidePayments(lista.data("index"),$(this).parent());
            });
        });

        
        function slidePayments(index, lista){
            var slide = lista.find("li");
            slide.hide();
            if(lista.hasClass("mci")){
                slide.slice(index*4,(index*4)+4).show();
                if (slide.length > index*4 && lista.find("li:visible").length == 4) {
                    lista.find(".rightControl").show();
                }
                if (lista.find("li:visible").length < 4) {
                    lista.find(".rightControl").hide();
                }
            }else{
                slide.slice(index*8,(index*8)+8).show();
                if (slide.length > index*8 &&lista.find("li:visible").length == 8) {
                    lista.find(".rightControl").show();
                }
                if (lista.find("li:visible").length < 8) {
                    lista.find(".rightControl").hide();
                }
            }
            if (index == 0) {
                lista.find(".leftControl").hide();
            }
            if(index > 0){
                lista.find(".leftControl").show();
            }
        }
